        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer22773257&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer22773257" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12802641820780749244">The only way I can describe what I didn't like about this book is with spoilers, so be wary...<br/><br/>The premise was my least liked plot--ever. Death "warrant" (sort of) was placed on Danika and her family by the gods in book #2 of this series. She morphed from sweet and innocent to believing--with a few courses in self-defense--she could kick the demons butt (Aeron) that was after her. The constant love/hate that went on between the h/h was annoying. Danika's agreement to act as Bait for the Hunters' </span>
  <span id="freeText12802641820780749244" style="display:none">The only way I can describe what I didn't like about this book is with spoilers, so be wary...<br /><br />The premise was my least liked plot--ever. Death "warrant" (sort of) was placed on Danika and her family by the gods in book #2 of this series. She morphed from sweet and innocent to believing--with a few courses in self-defense--she could kick the demons butt (Aeron) that was after her. The constant love/hate that went on between the h/h was annoying. Danika's agreement to act as Bait for the Hunters' had me not liking her. Reyes wants her, but afraid he'll ruin her/won't let her go/but keeps her at a distance/can't wait to see her...all this turns me right off a book. <br /><br />Black hair dye does not wash out in two shampoos! <br /><br />I hated the fact that Reyes had to have pain to experience pleasure. Big (BIG) sad face on that alone. His demon was pain. He jumped off a building to experience the pain of shattered bones while the others joked about hiding his internal organs--like they did an earlier time. Yuck.<br /><br />Top all that with the author using filler to re-tell what just happened was annoying, imo. The author did a fine job refreshing events in earlier books. I've read a "few books" since and it was good having the details again. But, there was no need to re-explain what I just read in this book. Argh!<br /><br />Throughout most of <i>The Darkest Pleasure</i>, Paris (demon: promiscuity) story gets set up. For me, doubtful I will continue this series. I'm so burned out on paranormal books that they really have to be exceptional to hold my interest and a book about a man who can't have sex with the same person twice (male/female) is a another big turn-off for me. If I don't like the characters, I'm not going to like the book.<br /><br />Bummer</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13127896726694317302">This paranormal series have completely rocked my world.I am so awed and emotionally invested in these books that my mind becomes cloudy once i finished this book."The Darkest Pleasure" is the third book in the "Lords of the Underworld" series and follows the fierce runaway beauty Danika Ford and her dark irresistible captor Reyes who is possessed by the demon of Pain.Another adventure of blissful steamy romance between two soulmates who don`t want to crave each other.We met Reyes and Danika in t</span>
  <span id="freeText13127896726694317302" style="display:none">This paranormal series have completely rocked my world.I am so awed and emotionally invested in these books that my mind becomes cloudy once i finished this book."The Darkest Pleasure" is the third book in the "Lords of the Underworld" series and follows the fierce runaway beauty Danika Ford and her dark irresistible captor Reyes who is possessed by the demon of Pain.Another adventure of blissful steamy romance between two soulmates who don`t want to crave each other.We met Reyes and Danika in the first book,and haven´t forgotten the loud fireworks between these two.Their agonizing romance consumed me!<br /><br />Danika Ford was a headcracker,very brave but also vulnerable.She was running all the time and striving to survive-all the while worrying about her family knowing Aeron is after all of their blood.Her torment and the way she gets torn between Reyes and her family is understandable to me,while many readers hated her for it.She did work for the Hunters for a while,but she never betrayed Reyes,never let herself go that far,and for that i forgave her.She loved Reyes without knowing,and Reyes...the besotted man he is forgave her easily.Ahhh i just loved him so much that i wanted him for myself.!I also found it so interesting that she is the Eye and hold a very powerful gift of visions into the past and future.<br /><br />Reyes the keeper of Pain was one tortured,dark,rugged,mouthwateringly smexay hero i wanted to devour!His dark soul sang to me and his irreversible devotion,caring,loyalty,adoration,fascination and love for Danika was mindblowingly irresistible!I love myself a smitten,possessive and jealous hero willing to do everything for his heroine!He was very self-destructive because of his demon who actually grew on me.The demon could be fun at times despite his crave for pain.I love him as a warrior and find him totally fascinating as a passionate lover.The sex-scenes were...GOD DO I NEED SAY MORE!Hot and steamy as i love them!His bromance with his friends tugs at my heart,he cares much for them and i was so touched when at the start he envied the closeness Lucien had with Anya which Maddox also have with Ashlyn.He wished that he had that with Danika,instead of her hating him all the time.However,he still succeeded in stealing her heart and i am so happy for the deserving happy ending for both of them!<br /><br />William have moved in to the Fortress and i am so loving his humor.Paris almost choose to have his mate Sienna back instead of saving Aeron from the bloodthirst,i actually understood why.My heart cried out for Paris,having to sleep with new woman everytime everyday just to not get weak is almost crushing him because ever since meeting Sienna he hates it.His soul is pining for only her.One thing i came to understand is that for these Lords,their soulmates will always come first in their hearts.But in the end,he knowingly (but with grief) made the right decision.I am so longing for Sienna to get resurrected from the death so she can take care of Paris starved golden heart.I also get to meet Gilly for the first time,she sounds like an interesting character!Now i am ready to read Sabin`s story,ahhh his darkness just calls to my soul!</span>

<div id="review_91154446" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/91154446" />
    <a title="Tracy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3040429-tracy"><img alt="Tracy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1265753341p2/3040429.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/91154446?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tracy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tracy" href="/user/show/3040429-tracy">Tracy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3040429-tracy?shelf=z-2010">z-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3040429-tracy?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer91154446" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10149594036067304113">4 ½ stars<br/><br/><b>Darkest Pleasure</b> quickly just became my favorite book of the Lords of the Underworld series thus far. While I liked the first two books and planned to finish the series sometime this year, after reading this book I will definitely read the next two books this month.<br/><br/>Why am I now dying to finish the series? <br/><br/>First, I felt like I got to know some of the other warriors much better. There was also more interplay between one another. With the Budapest group, you really see the bond that they s</span>
  <span id="freeText10149594036067304113" style="display:none">4 ½ stars<br /><br /><b>Darkest Pleasure</b> quickly just became my favorite book of the Lords of the Underworld series thus far. While I liked the first two books and planned to finish the series sometime this year, after reading this book I will definitely read the next two books this month.<br /><br />Why am I now dying to finish the series? <br /><br />First, I felt like I got to know some of the other warriors much better. There was also more interplay between one another. With the Budapest group, you really see the bond that they share and the personal sacrifices they make for their fellow “brother.” Also, the two factions (Budapest &amp; Greece) begin rekindling their bond, fighting alongside and poking fun with one another. Though the other warriors got good airtime, I never felt like I was missing out on the story of Danika and Reyes, which coincidently was also great. All together, I just got the warm fuzzies and can’t wait read more about each warrior, particularly Sabin, Gideon, Torin and Misery. <br /><br />Second, this book provided great color on the history of the Lords and the dynamics of their interactions with the Greeks/Titans. Also, the introduction of a new enemy stirs up the pot and creates some anticipation for what will happen next. <br /><br />Speaking of what will happen next, I must go get <b>The Darkest Whisper</b>.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10149594036067304113" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_153652983" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/153652983" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/153652983?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=pararnormal-romance">pararnormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=lords-of-the-underworld">lords-of-the-underworld</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer153652983" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6436542631733299865">There really is someone out there for everyone. Even an immortal warrior, who can only find pleasure in bone-wrenching pain. Reyes is one of the Lords of the Underworld. Each immortal carries within him a demon which escaped from hell. Reyes carries Pain, and longs to hurt himself and others. He cuts himself, breaks his own bones, whatever it takes to cause pain and soothe the beast inside of him.<br/><br/>We knew Danika was the woman for him back in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/476543.The_Darkest_Night__Lords_of_the_Underworld___1_' title='The Darkest Night (Lords of the Underworld, #1) by Gena Showalter' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Darkest Night</a>. But he resisted his feelings for her</span>
  <span id="freeText6436542631733299865" style="display:none">There really is someone out there for everyone. Even an immortal warrior, who can only find pleasure in bone-wrenching pain. Reyes is one of the Lords of the Underworld. Each immortal carries within him a demon which escaped from hell. Reyes carries Pain, and longs to hurt himself and others. He cuts himself, breaks his own bones, whatever it takes to cause pain and soothe the beast inside of him.<br /><br />We knew Danika was the woman for him back in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/476543.The_Darkest_Night__Lords_of_the_Underworld___1_" title="The Darkest Night (Lords of the Underworld, #1) by Gena Showalter" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Night</a>. But he resisted his feelings for her because he was afraid his demon would taint her. Well, that and the fact that his best bud Aeron is fighting a Titan-induced compulsion to kill her. But three books later, Reyes is finally giving in to his desires. Danika's life has been turned upside down since she came under the Lords' radar. She's been on the run, hiding from Lords and Hunters alike. She's been forced to harden herself, to live in poverty. And in the end, it's not enough. Hunters catch up with her and that leads Reyes back into her life, because he must save her.<br /><br />The couple is thrown together, as Reyes vows to protect Danika and she works to find the rest of her missing family. And even though they're both fighting it, their attraction is undeniable. Now, I know there are a lot of people out there who find pleasure in some degree of pain. And skirting that line can be a turn-on. It just isn't for me. And that put a big damper on the book, because, obviously, Reyes IS Pain. There is one particularly disturbing scene in the bathroom with Reyes and a knife... Suffice it to say, it icked me out.<br /><br />And yet, despite this, it was a good book. Even with the pain thing, the book was rich in sexual tension, which Showalter plays like a violin. The great world building continues. I felt so much anguish for Paris... sympathy for all the lonely Lords, each with such burdens to bear. These books are sexy romances, but they're also more. In short order, Showalter has helped us grow emotionally invested in this immortal family. And the ongoing story arc is entertaining, exciting, and always surprising. 4 stars. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6436542631733299865" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText48357512510100976" style="display:none"><b>★★★ 3 STARS!</b><br /><br />This is the least favorite LOTU but have an interesting story. Pleasure. Yeah, sorry for my perv mind. <div id="review_100617602" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/100617602" />
    <a title="Gokce ~Muslin Myst~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst"><img alt="Gokce ~Muslin Myst~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365363362p2/2855030.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/100617602?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gokce ~Muslin Myst~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gokce ~Muslin Myst~" href="/user/show/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst">Gokce ~Muslin Myst~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=books-that-own-me">books-that-own-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=race-immortal-warriors">race-immortal-warriors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=2010">2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=books-i-ll-never-part-with">books-i-ll-never-part-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2855030-gokce-muslin-myst?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer100617602&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer100617602" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17838760542419677302">With every single book I read of this series I love it even more. <br/>This book is about Reyes, keeper of the demon Pain, who fell for the human woman Danika who was ordered in the first book to be killed by Aeron, keeper of Wrath. <br/>Nicely handled story, gotta say. I was very curious about Pain's story, about how he would handle his constant need for cutting himself with the romance. And there was a point I thought the story would go into the BDSM waters, which I'm not really all that happy to read a</span>
  <span id="freeText17838760542419677302" style="display:none">With every single book I read of this series I love it even more. <br />This book is about Reyes, keeper of the demon Pain, who fell for the human woman Danika who was ordered in the first book to be killed by Aeron, keeper of Wrath. <br />Nicely handled story, gotta say. I was very curious about Pain's story, about how he would handle his constant need for cutting himself with the romance. And there was a point I thought the story would go into the BDSM waters, which I'm not really all that happy to read about, but Gena Showalter handled it very nicely. I think this book was the most emotional one so far, with Reyes' dilemma about his need for pain and the safekeeping of the woman he loved. Since he's possessed by the demon of Pain, every woman he's ever slept with somehow turned to pain themselves, either by hurting themselves or others and so he's afraid he might corrupt Danika as well who he considers to be an angel with a gentle heart. And then there's Danika's dilemma, her desperate need to save her family from certain death and the man she's somehow craved from the first moment she saw him. The two made a good couple I thought. Danika is young and determined but not at all cocky that she might annoy you. Far from it. The way she handles the situation with her family and the Hunters forces her to make mistakes which makes her all the more believable. And I could totally relate to her dilemma about her family.<br /><br />Another thing why ı loved this book was Aeron. He seems to just suffer so much. More than the others because of his bloodlust. And deep inside he's the warrior who doesn't want to hurt anyone but he's left without a choice. This guy couldn't need his book any sooner. I felt for him. Strongly.<br /><br />I can't help but say how glad I was when Paris picked Aeron over Sienna, who he was -by some miracle- able to get a hard for more than once. I would be really disappointed if it was the other way around. Bros before hoes.<br /><br />We were introduced more to the point of view of Sabin, who has the next book. And I sure wonder about that. Again, I love the fact that this guy passes out upon lying. I wish we could read that at least once.<br /><br />And then finally, the one constant point that I believe I'll include in every single book's review of this series; the freakin' awesome interaction between the heroines with the other guys. I absolutely love the fact that they are so good together, as friends, and they make sandwiches for each other and hug each other when comfort needed. So adorable. And it's good that even though these are all alpha males, they are aware of common behaviour :) A 5 star read all the way.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17838760542419677302" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0bhgzQabBS/4hpaFOfA8vS3nai8+0ML8trAnRQfDN/GZXLdJlnTLtHx7QO9GGVNKIrUO9jk5ipvhnIw5SChnmQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('58Fx2eSBSQ0irDWsV1WAac3zXT+IOEqP6ynDbr/MEfGvJaZddG6HlqZR48YovO+ewqE55o/RAui8BWgS8CdBmQ==')})
  }
